#Volokar
e_volokar = {
	color = { 8 170 26 }

	capital = c_cahillion # Cahillion
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = culture:chellan
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
}
